namespace = VFS
province_event = {
	id = VFS.1
	hide_window = yes 

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		878 = { add_province_modifier = { name = religous_demographics duration = -1 } }
		878 = { set_variable = { which = miaphysite_var value = 30 } }
		878 = { set_variable = { which = kemetic_pagan_var value = 60 } }
		878 = { set_variable = { which = sunni_var value = 10 } }
	}	
}
province_event = {
	id = VFS.2
	hide_window = yes 

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		878 = { change_variable = { which = miaphysite_var value = -30 } }
		878 = { change_variable = { which = kemetic_pagan_var value = 30 } }
	}	
}
